</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p7204610"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p7204610"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p7204610"></a>Yes</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p46702574"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p46702574"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p46702574"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p24812117"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p24812117"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p24812117"></a>Name must be unique within a namespace. Is required when creating resources, although some resources may allow a client to request the generation of an appropriate name automatically. Name is primarily intended for creation idempotence and configuration definition. Cannot be updated.</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p21982467"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p21982467"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p21982467"></a>0 characters &lt; name length ≤ 253 characters.</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p63624481"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p63624481"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p63624481"></a>The name must be a regular expression [a-z0-9]([-a-z0-9]*[a-z0-9])?.</p>
</td>

</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aa797d310fa1f45eaa77f717bfc84c893"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aa797d310fa1f45eaa77f717bfc84c893"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aa797d310fa1f45eaa77f717bfc84c893"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p298114516322"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p298114516322"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p298114516322"></a>The name of the cluster which the object belongs to. This is used to distinguish resources with same name and namespace in different clusters. This field is not set anywhere right now and apiserver is going to ignore it if set in create or update request.</p>
<div class="note" id="note1635112319154"><a name="note1635112319154"></a><a name="note1635112319154"></a><span class="notetitle"> 说明： </span><div class="notebody"><p id="p4939113611513"><a name="p4939113611513"></a><a name="p4939113611513"></a>除了evs卷，其他类型的卷不支持</p>
</div></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_r0a22491267344f6798654cf01dbaa6f3"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p576283116341"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p576283116341"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p576283116341"></a>initializers</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a0314e1962ef847328758d9fc451ec0c4"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a0314e1962ef847328758d9fc451ec0c4"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a0314e1962ef847328758d9fc451ec0c4"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aad3f959e5e404dff95bb6244adc0d228"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aad3f959e5e404dff95bb6244adc0d228"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aad3f959e5e404dff95bb6244adc0d228"></a><a href="#zh-cn_topic_0083857342_t693768b66dfa47239c0f155ad4dd18e8">initializers</a> object</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_af039aab6875e4fc4abd420dd5f11ee95"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_af039aab6875e4fc4abd420dd5f11ee95"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_af039aab6875e4fc4abd420dd5f11ee95"></a>An initializer is a controller which enforces some system invariant at object creation time. This field is a list of initializers that have not yet acted on this object. If nil or empty, this object has been completely initialized. Otherwise, the object is considered uninitialized and is hidden (in list/watch and get calls) from clients that haven't explicitly asked to observe uninitialized objects. When an object is created, the system will populate this list with the current set of initializers. Only privileged users may set or modify this list. Once it is empty, it may not be modified further by any user.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row35749425"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p10022287"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p10022287"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p10022287"></a>generateName</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p6498885"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p6498885"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p6498885"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p56647676"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p56647676"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p56647676"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p25059035"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p25059035"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p25059035"></a>An optional prefix used by the server to generate a unique name ONLY IF the Name field has not been provided. If this field is used, the name returned to the client will be different from the name passed. This value will also be combined with a unique suffix. The provided value has the same validation rules as the Name field, and may be truncated by the length of the suffix required to make the value unique on the server.</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p24204730"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p24204730"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p24204730"></a>If this field is specified and the generated name exists, the server will NOT return a 409. Instead, it will either return 201 Created or 500 with Reason ServerTimeout indicating a unique name could not be found in the time allotted, and the client should retry (optionally after the time indicated in the Retry-After header).</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p16515979"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p16515979"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p16515979"></a>Applied only if Name is not specified.</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p14426089"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p14426089"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p14426089"></a>0 characters &lt; generated name length ≤ 253 characters.</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p62725940"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p62725940"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p62725940"></a>The generated name must be a regular expression [a-z0-9]([-a-z0-9]*[a-z0-9])?.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row27662549"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p26073957"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p26073957"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p26073957"></a>namespace</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p31615745"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p31615745"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p31615745"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p10738578"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p10738578"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p10738578"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p64518528"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p64518528"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p64518528"></a>Namespace defines the space within each name must be unique. An empty namespace is equivalent to the "default" namespace, but "default" is the canonical representation. Not all objects are required to be scoped to a namespace - the value of this field for those objects will be empty. Must be a DNS_LABEL. Cannot be updated.</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p43795845"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p43795845"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p43795845"></a>0 characters &lt; namespace length ≤ 63 characters.</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p58618290"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p58618290"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p58618290"></a>The namespace must be a regular expression [a-z0-9]([-a-z0-9]*[a-z0-9])?.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row57802569"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p51496476"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p51496476"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p51496476"></a>selfLink</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p10465065"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p10465065"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p10465065"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p42363926"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p42363926"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p42363926"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p8925963"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p8925963"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p8925963"></a>A URL representing this object. Populated by the system. Read-only.</p>
<div class="note" id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note13224809"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note13224809"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note13224809"></a><span class="notetitle"> 说明： </span><div class="notebody"><p class="textintable" id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p51914417"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p51914417"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p51914417"></a>This field is automatically generated. Do not assign any value to this field. Otherwise, API calls would fail.</p>
</div></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row64576574"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p63319983"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p63319983"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p63319983"></a>uid</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p28645030"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p28645030"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p28645030"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p38546056"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p38546056"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p38546056"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p35222847"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p35222847"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p35222847"></a>UID is the unique in time and space value for this object. It is typically generated by the server on successful creation of a resource and is not allowed to change on PUT operations. Populated by the system. Read-only.</p>
<div class="note" id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note48570174"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note48570174"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note48570174"></a><span class="notetitle"> 说明： </span><div class="notebody"><p class="textintable" id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p34478387"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p34478387"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p34478387"></a>This field is automatically generated. Do not assign any value to this field. Otherwise, API calls would fail.</p>
</div></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row41870031"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p36029352"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p36029352"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p36029352"></a>resourceVersion</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p32696434"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p32696434"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p32696434"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p31165525"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p31165525"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p31165525"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p41379576"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p41379576"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p41379576"></a>An opaque value that represents the internal version of this object that can be used by clients to determine when objects have changed. May be used for optimistic concurrency, change detection, and the watch operation on a resource or set of resources. Clients must treat these values as opaque and passed unmodified back to the server. They may only be valid for a particular resource or set of resources. Populated by the system. Read-only. Value must be treated as opaque by clients.</p>
<div class="note" id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note36871865"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note36871865"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note36871865"></a><span class="notetitle"> 说明： </span><div class="notebody"><p class="textintable" id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p63411331"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p63411331"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p63411331"></a>This field is automatically generated. Do not assign any value to this field. Otherwise, API calls would fail.</p>
</div></div>
</td>

</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p31998689"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p31998689"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p31998689"></a>No</p>

It is not guaranteed to be set in happens-before order across separate operations. Clients may not set this value. It is represented in RFC3339 form and is in UTC. Populated by the system. Read-only. Null for lists.</p>
<div class="note" id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note40544022"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note40544022"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_note40544022"></a><span class="notetitle"> 说明： </span><div class="notebody"><p class="textintable" id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p29351881"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p29351881"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p29351881"></a>This field is automatically generated. <tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row62840338"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p56902578"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p56902578"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p56902578"></a>deletionTimestamp</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p45706078"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p45706078"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p45706078"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p11204863"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p11204863"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p11204863"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p35178749"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p35178749"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p35178749"></a>RFC 3339 date and time at which this resource will be deleted. This field is set by the server when a graceful deletion is requested by the user, and is not directly settable by a client. The resource will be deleted (no longer visible from resource lists, and not reachable by name) after the time in this field. Once set, this value may not be unset or be set further into the future, although it may be shortened or the resource may be deleted prior to this time. For example, a user may request that a pod is deleted in 30 seconds. The Kubelet will react by sending a graceful termination signal to the containers in the pod. Once the resource is deleted in the API, the Kubelet will send a hard termination signal to the container. If not set, graceful deletion of the object has not been requested. Populated by the system when a graceful deletion is requested. Read-only.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row48173290"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p9722430"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p9722430"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p9722430"></a>deletionGracePeriodSeconds</p>

</td>

<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p783254124017"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p783254124017"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p783254124017"></a>Pending is a list of initializers that must execute in order before this object is visible. When the last pending initializer is removed, and no failing result is set, the initializers struct will be set to nil and the object is considered as initialized and visible to all clients.</p>

<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row35965948"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p27560669"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p27560669"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p27560669"></a>terminationGracePeriodSeconds</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p17821682"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p17821682"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p17821682"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p34270115"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p34270115"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p34270115"></a>Integer</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p24415962"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p24415962"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p24415962"></a>Optional duration in seconds the pod needs to terminate gracefully. May be decreased in delete request. Value must be a non-negative integer. The value zero indicates delete immediately. If this value is nil, the default grace period will be used instead. The grace period is the duration in seconds after the processes running in the pod are sent a termination signal and the time when the processes are forcibly halted with a kill signal. Set this value longer than the expected cleanup time for your process. Defaults to 30 seconds.</p>
</td>
</tr>

If not specified, the pod will be dispatched by default scheduler.</p>
<div class="note" id="note480114232111"><a name="note480114232111"></a><a name="note480114232111"></a><span class="notetitle"> 说明： </span><div class="notebody"><p id="p1171021017215"><a name="p1171021017215"></a><a name="p1171021017215"></a>不支持设置指定scheduler name</p>
</div></div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row61552586"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p19703558"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p19703558"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p19703558"></a>nodeName</p>

<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p52484326"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p52484326"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p52484326"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p23371986"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p23371986"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p23371986"></a>String</p>

<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p14082739"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p14082739"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p14082739"></a>A request to schedule this pod onto a specific node. If it is non-empty, the scheduler simply schedules this pod onto that node, assuming that it fits resource requirements.</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p59635795"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p59635795"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p59635795"></a>0 characters &lt; node name length ≤ 253 characters.</p>

<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_rec439ba9fa81470ca61ec1feb17426c2"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a948d075274df4649b1308262855bb333"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a948d075274df4649b1308262855bb333"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a948d075274df4649b1308262855bb333"></a>initContainers</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a9840c0cdc60e4f27a2f8a9fc65f2993b"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a9840c0cdc60e4f27a2f8a9fc65f2993b"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a9840c0cdc60e4f27a2f8a9fc65f2993b"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aa16fa8ef21a146a2a6b3255bf7c9cb68"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aa16fa8ef21a146a2a6b3255bf7c9cb68"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aa16fa8ef21a146a2a6b3255bf7c9cb68"></a><a href="#zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_table56770522">containers</a> object</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p919131811365"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p919131811365"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p919131811365"></a></p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a110a7effef0d40909e8825d1b5aa8fd6"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a110a7effef0d40909e8825d1b5aa8fd6"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a110a7effef0d40909e8825d1b5aa8fd6"></a>List of initialization containers belonging to the pod. Init containers are executed in order prior to containers being started. If any init container fails, the pod is considered to have failed and is handled according to its restartPolicy. The name for an init container or normal container must be unique among all containers. Init containers may not have Lifecycle actions, Readiness probes, or Liveness probes. The resourceRequirements of an init container are taken into account during scheduling by finding the highest request/limit for each resource type, and then using the max of of that value or the sum of the normal containers. Limits are applied to init containers in a similar fashion. Init containers cannot currently be added or removed.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_redb4f46250a14dfdace6ba9146215eea"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a2866c93cae894fcd9f6074f68e56fc45"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a2866c93cae894fcd9f6074f68e56fc45"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a2866c93cae894fcd9f6074f68e56fc45"></a>hostname</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p124944208284"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p124944208284"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p124944208284"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="20%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a69e659fee8294b40a0b99f3d621d111e"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a69e659fee8294b40a0b99f3d621d111e"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a69e659fee8294b40a0b99f3d621d111e"></a>String</p>
</td>

<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a0e566aca6835457b9b6e742b829585c5"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a0e566aca6835457b9b6e742b829585c5"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a0e566aca6835457b9b6e742b829585c5"></a>List of sources to populate environment variables in the container. The keys defined within a source must be a C_IDENTIFIER. All invalid keys will be reported as an event when the container is starting. When a key exists in multiple sources, the value associated with the last source will take precedence. Values defined by an Env with a duplicate key will take precedence. Cannot be updated.</p>
</td>
</tr>

</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.306069393060696%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p45106256"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p45106256"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p45106256"></a>A flag indicating whether this container should allocate a buffer for stdin in the container runtime. If this is not set, reads from stdin in the container will always result in EOF. Default is false.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row3303123"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21.23787621237876%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p66226448"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p66226448"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p66226448"></a>stdinOnce</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p62742061"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p62742061"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p62742061"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.71802819718028%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p48942162"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p48942162"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p48942162"></a>Boolean</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.306069393060696%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p4892200"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p4892200"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p4892200"></a>A flag indicating whether the container runtime should close the stdin channel after it has been opened by a single attach. When stdin is true, the stdin stream will remain open across multiple attach sessions. If stdinOnce is set to true, stdin is opened on container start, is empty until the first client attaches to stdin, and then remains open and accepts data until the client disconnects, at which time stdin is closed and remains closed until the container is restarted. If this flag is false, a container process that reads from stdin will never receive an EOF. Default is false.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row44029805"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21.23787621237876%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p9644430"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p9644430"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p9644430"></a>tty</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p43001397"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p43001397"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p43001397"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.71802819718028%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p60561095"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p60561095"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p60561095"></a>Boolean</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.306069393060696%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p6501678"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p6501678"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p6501678"></a>A flag indicating whether this container should allocate a TTY for itself, also requires 'stdin' to be true. Default is false.</p>
</td>
</tr>

</table>

**表 24**  securityContext字段数据结构说明

<a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_table41172652"></a>
<table><thead align="left"><tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_row48603320"><th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21.23787621237876%" id="mcps1.2.5.1.1"><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p44554846"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p44554846"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p44554846"></a>参数</p>
</th>
<th class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" id="mcps1.2.5.1.2"><p id="p05401132450"><a name="p05401132450"></a><a name="p05401132450"></a>是否必选</p>

If true, the Kubelet will validate the image at runtime to ensure that it does not run as UID 0 (root) and fail to start the container if it does. If unset or false, no such validation will be performed. May also be set in SecurityContext. If set in both SecurityContext and PodSecurityContext, the value specified in SecurityContext takes precedence.</p>

</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.28607139286072%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p39281331"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p39281331"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p39281331"></a>Variable references $(VAR_NAME) are expanded using the previous defined environment variables in the container and any service environment variables. If a variable cannot be resolved, the reference in the input string will be unchanged. The $(VAR_NAME) syntax can be escaped with a double $$, for example, $$(VAR_NAME). Escaped references will never be expanded, regardless of whether the variable exists or not. Defaults to "".</p>
</td>
</tr>

<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p64957389"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p64957389"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p64957389"></a>No</p>

<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.28607139286072%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p44147557"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p44147557"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p44147557"></a>Run container in privileged mode. Processes in privileged containers are essentially equivalent to root on the host.</p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ad0f395031b78446b9cecf8c77a90c6c7"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ad0f395031b78446b9cecf8c77a90c6c7"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ad0f395031b78446b9cecf8c77a90c6c7"></a>Value:</p>

<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a160b663a2dc2401b9edbaaa2e7bc0a51"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a160b663a2dc2401b9edbaaa2e7bc0a51"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a160b663a2dc2401b9edbaaa2e7bc0a51"></a>Default: false.</p>
<div class="note" id="note137171419219"><a name="note137171419219"></a><a name="note137171419219"></a><span class="notetitle"> 说明： </span><div class="notebody"><p id="p1742015212214"><a name="p1742015212214"></a><a name="p1742015212214"></a>Run container in privileged mode</p>

Defaults to user specified in image metadata if unspecified. May also be set in PodSecurityContext. If set in both SecurityContext and PodSecurityContext, the value specified in SecurityContext takes precedence.</p>
</td>

<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p11230212"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p11230212"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p11230212"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p37231957"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p37231957"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p37231957"></a>Boolean</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.28607139286072%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p62998572"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p62998572"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p62998572"></a>Indicates that the container must run as a non-root user. If true, the Kubelet will validate the image at runtime to ensure that it does not run as UID 0 (root) and fail to start the container if it does. If unset or false, no such validation will be performed. May also be set in PodSecurityContext. If set in both SecurityContext and PodSecurityContext, the value specified in SecurityContext takes precedence.</p>

<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.28607139286072%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p756946154020"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p756946154020"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p756946154020"></a></p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_af7c8361d6e2c4e0d8b3e4faeb4d5efa1"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_af7c8361d6e2c4e0d8b3e4faeb4d5efa1"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_af7c8361d6e2c4e0d8b3e4faeb4d5efa1"></a>The scheduler will prefer to schedule pods to nodes that satisfy the affinity expressions specified by this field, but it may choose a node that violates one or more of the expressions. The node that is most preferred is the one with the greatest sum of weights, i.e. for each node that meets all of the scheduling requirements (resource request, requiredDuringScheduling affinity expressions, etc.), compute a sum by iterating through the elements of this field and adding "weight" to the sum if the node matches the corresponding matchExpressions; the node(s) with the highest sum are the most preferred.</p>

If the operator is Gt or Lt, the values array must have a single element, which will be interpreted as an integer. This array is replaced during a strategic merge patch.</p>

</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a78a7b67fbb354640b1a61ce75775f68c"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a78a7b67fbb354640b1a61ce75775f68c"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a78a7b67fbb354640b1a61ce75775f68c"></a>No</p>

<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ae01ce0633e4d4d26a81db0ea0e699909"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ae01ce0633e4d4d26a81db0ea0e699909"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ae01ce0633e4d4d26a81db0ea0e699909"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.28607139286072%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a35464781ddc3479fb2ffda6d5270479f"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a35464781ddc3479fb2ffda6d5270479f"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a35464781ddc3479fb2ffda6d5270479f"></a></p>
<p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a63409f93c5914d3bb8b5a23e7ca7dec4"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a63409f93c5914d3bb8b5a23e7ca7dec4"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a63409f93c5914d3bb8b5a23e7ca7dec4"></a>This pod should be co-located (affinity) or not co-located (anti-affinity) with the pods matching the labelSelector in the specified namespaces, where co-located is defined as running on a node whose value of the label with key topologyKey matches that of any node on which any of the selected pods is running. For PreferredDuringScheduling pod anti-affinity, empty topologyKey is interpreted as "all topologies" ("all topologies" here means all the topologyKeys indicated by scheduler command-line argument --failure-domains); for affinity and for RequiredDuringScheduling pod anti-affinity, empty topologyKey is not allowed.</p>
</td>

</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_r797f7eda1b8a43478b7f11e2bb1a40eb"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21.23787621237876%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p32716155532"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p32716155532"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p32716155532"></a>operator</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_acce1b03e05d14c83b0bf3bfdf9a2128b"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_acce1b03e05d14c83b0bf3bfdf9a2128b"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_acce1b03e05d14c83b0bf3bfdf9a2128b"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aa48704748d7a4e0e95d5fc774267a1a6"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aa48704748d7a4e0e95d5fc774267a1a6"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_aa48704748d7a4e0e95d5fc774267a1a6"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.28607139286072%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a2284fb7491f84bb6b38755643e38bea3"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a2284fb7491f84bb6b38755643e38bea3"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a2284fb7491f84bb6b38755643e38bea3"></a>Operator represents a key's relationship to the value. Valid operators are Exists and Equal. Defaults to Equal. Exists is equivalent to wildcard for value, so that a pod can tolerate all taints of a particular category.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_r50f36b5ece3849dfa0038a90992a0c85"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21.23787621237876%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ad85a2d91cf33475fb5c20b917e14b8ab"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ad85a2d91cf33475fb5c20b917e14b8ab"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ad85a2d91cf33475fb5c20b917e14b8ab"></a>tolerationSeconds</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a245233da09684628b3fcb02fac899ac2"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a245233da09684628b3fcb02fac899ac2"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a245233da09684628b3fcb02fac899ac2"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ab8d3681c1178457da11997fcfba2c8bd"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ab8d3681c1178457da11997fcfba2c8bd"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ab8d3681c1178457da11997fcfba2c8bd"></a>Integer</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.28607139286072%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a88981a0716f1431fb358f265ebae85c0"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a88981a0716f1431fb358f265ebae85c0"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a88981a0716f1431fb358f265ebae85c0"></a>TolerationSeconds represents the period of time the toleration (which must be of effect NoExecute, otherwise this field is ignored) tolerates the taint. By default, it is not set, which means tolerate the taint forever (do not evict). Zero and negative values will be treated as 0 (evict immediately) by the system.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_r46e8b1b7955641419eb9289aae325a14"><td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="21.23787621237876%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.1 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p57474218533"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p57474218533"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_zh-cn_topic_0079614925_p57474218533"></a>value</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.2 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ac24d00ef334349f395e758e9a6c23b88"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ac24d00ef334349f395e758e9a6c23b88"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ac24d00ef334349f395e758e9a6c23b88"></a>No</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="19.73802619738026%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.3 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ab3d88d4182a4411691da1b38a1290274"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ab3d88d4182a4411691da1b38a1290274"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_ab3d88d4182a4411691da1b38a1290274"></a>String</p>
</td>
<td class="cellrowborder" valign="top" width="39.28607139286072%" headers="mcps1.2.5.1.4 "><p id="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a290f5b8ad7de4a29af299bd869e41334"><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a290f5b8ad7de4a29af299bd869e41334"></a><a name="zh-cn_topic_0083857342_a290f5b8ad7de4a29af299bd869e41334"></a>Value is the taint value the toleration matches to. If the operator is Exists, the value should be empty, otherwise just a regular string.</p>
</td>
</tr>
